// JavaScript Document
function toggle(classname){
	$(classname).hover(function() {$(this).addClass("hover");}, function() {$(this).removeClass("hover");});
}

$(document).ready(function(){	
	toggle(".haschild");
	toggle(".sec-time span");
	toggle(".prifilter span");
	toggle(".header-search input");
	toggle(".filterRange");
	toggle(".header-search input");
	toggle(".p-help");

});

var alldt = $("#relateSelect>dt");
function showNear(dt){
    alldt.each(function(){
        if(this == dt) {$(this).next("dd").show();$(this).addClass("select");}
        else {$(this).next("dd").hide();$(this).removeClass("select");}
    });
}
alldt.each(function(){
    $(this).click(function(){showNear(this);}).hover(function(){showNear(this);});
});

showNear(alldt[0]);

  
//信息hover
boot.require('dom, anim.hover', function(Frame, dom, hover){
	var cc = dom.get('infolist'),
	    trs = cc.getElementsByTagName('tr');
	Frame.each(trs, function(item){
		hover.bind(item, 'bg');
	});
});

$(".selector").each(function(){
	$(this).hover(function(){$(this).addClass("hover")},function(){$(this).removeClass("hover")});
});

<script>
$(function(){
	$('.yuyue_vertop .click_btn').click(function(){
		$_haveImg=$(this).parents('.yuyue_vertop').find('.content_jumpDiv .have_ewm img');
		if($_haveImg){
			$_haveImg.attr('src',$_haveImg.attr('_imgsrc'));
		}
		$('.yuyue_vertop').css('z-index',99);
		$(this).parents('.yuyue_vertop').css('z-index',999);
		var tel = $(this).parents('.yuyue_vertop').find('.guishudi').attr("tel");
		var tel_city= $(this).parents('.yuyue_vertop').find('.guishudi');
		$.ajax({
            type: "GET",
            url:"http://huangye.api.58.com/phonearea/?phone="+tel,
            dataType: "jsonp",
            jsonp:"callback",
            callback:"aaa",
            success: function(data) {
				var phonearea = data.area;
				if(phonearea!=null && phonearea!=""){
					tel_city.html("归属地("+data.area+")");
				}                
            }
        })
		$('.content_jumpDiv').fadeOut('fast');
		$(this).parents('.yuyue_vertop').find('.content_jumpDiv').fadeIn("slow");		
	})
	$('.yuyue_vertop .close_btn').click(function(){
		$('.yuyue_vertop').css('z-index',99);
		$('.content_jumpDiv').fadeOut('slow')
	})
})
</script>
